易混词汇: address, greet, salute, hail, <b>welcome</b> 均有“欢迎，致敬，致意，招呼”之意。
				<span class="stips">  </span>				<div class="snt_info"><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=address">address</a>: 侧重打招呼的方式或指所使用的称谓。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=greet">greet</a>: 常指友好而热诚地欢迎。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=salute">salute</a>: 正式用词，指用敬礼、亲吻或挥帽等动作向他人致意或问候，尤指以某种礼节欢迎某人。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=hail">hail</a>: 主要指怀着敬意欢迎某人，侧重欢快轻松和嘈杂。也指隔得较远的高声招呼。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=welcome">welcome</a>: 多指热情的官方的或正式的迎接或欢迎，但也指一般的欢迎。

	 <div id="sponeLeft">
		<div id="etitle"> 
						<span id="swTitle">
			Public Spending  			</span>
					</div><!-- end etitle -->

		<div id="sponeLeftT" style="width: 100%; overflow: hidden; outline: none;" tabindex="0">			 
			<div id="contentsW">

				<div id="contents">
																<div id="parahtml"><p id="p_1"><span id="s_0">If you want to know how I spend my money, go to Blippy.com--each time I make a purchase on my credit card, the amount I've spent and the name of the place I've spent it automatically pop up on this weird new site.</span><span id="s_1"> Why would any sane person volunteer to publicize that information?</span><span id="s_2"> Philip Kaplan, a technology entrepreneur and one of Blippy's co-founders, hazards a guess: "To tell people--friends, acquaintances, maybe even strangers--a little bit more about you.</span><span id="s_3">"I had a different theory.</span><span id="s_4"> If scads of people could see and comment on what I was buying, maybe I would be shamed into spending less.</span><span id="s_5"> Could there be a practical use for the exhibitionism and groupthink of social networking?</span><span id="s_6"> Location-centric sites like Foursquare encourage people to blast where they are and what they're buying.</span><span id="s_7"> But Blippy takes things to a new level, since information goes straight from point of purchase to website.</span><span id="s_8"> You don't have to push a single button; just agree to let Blippy broadcast the details that end up on your credit-card statement.</span><span id="s_9"> Marketers are constantly mining all sorts of consumer data, and Blippy--which has received seed money from big-name investors like Sequoia Capital and Twitter CEO Evan Williams--wants to help individuals start harnessing this kind of information too.</span><span id="s_10">Conversations on Blippy occasionally revolve around how people should spend less for things.</span><span id="s_11"> If you pay more than $29.99 a month for a gym membership, expect to hear about it.</span><span id="s_12"> But more often the comments are pro-purchase.</span><span id="s_13"> That's especially true when people opt to specify what they5re buying on sites such as Amazon, iTunes and Netflix (I like The Office too!).</span><span id="s_14">During my first month on Blippy, which was in beta until Jan. 14, my proclivity for eating at Mexican restaurants quickly became a topic of conversation among the strangers who started following me on the site.</span><span id="s_15"> As I scrolled through other users' purchases, I was reminded that most people sometimes go to grocery stores instead of eating out every night.</span><span id="s_16"> I noticed another Blippy member getting joshed, about how often charges showed up from a particular bar.</span><span id="s_17"> He bantered back that to avoid the appearance of a drinking problem, maybe he should switch to cash.</span><span id="s_18">I ran my cost-control theory by Kaplan, and he said it was interesting--but that he had witnessed his spending habits being swayed in the other direction.</span><span id="s_19"> On a recent trip to Bali, he battled with a friend over who would get to pay for dinner.</span><span id="s_20"> He wasn't being gracious.</span><span id="s_21"> He simply wanted the Blippy community to see that he was in a cool place.</span><span id="s_22">I, too, eventually found that sharing details about what I was buying only made me want to spend more.</span><span id="s_23"> With friends on New Year's Eve, I asked to be the one to purchase a bottle of champagne.</span><span id="s_24"> In an odd way, I felt I would be ringing in the New Year with my Blippy compatriots.</span></p></div>
								
												</div>				
			</div>			 
		</div><!-- end sponeLeftT -->

				<li class="error_trp snt_hx" content="maybe" cate="confusion">[学习提示]			
易混词汇: <b>maybe</b>, perhaps, possibly, probably 均有“或许，大概”之意。<strong>maybe</strong>是副词，表示“也许，可能”，用作状语。<strong>may be</strong>表示“可能是，也许是”，用作谓语。<br /> 
				<span class="stips">  </span>				<div class="snt_info"><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=maybe">maybe</a>: 普通用词，美国英语多用。指某事也许如此，含不能确定意味。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=perhaps">perhaps</a>: 普通用词，多用于英国，与maybe同义。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=possibly">possibly</a>: 指客观上潜存着发生某种变化的可能。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=probably">probably</a>: 一般指根据逻辑推理，估计有发生的可能，把握性较大，语气比possibly强。 				 				 
				 <div class="stips_fb">
				 <span class="tipsGood">好评</span> 
				 <span class="tipsBad">报错</span> 
				 <!--
				  
				 -->
				 </div>
				 				 
				</div>
				</li>
				 								  
				<li class="error_trp snt_hx" content="people" cate="i_suggest.word">[推荐表达]			
individuals/characters/folks/citizen与短语<b>people</b> 意思相近，individuals/characters/folks/citizen 更地道，推荐使用。
				<span class="stips">  </span>				<div class="snt_info">				 				 
				 <div class="stips_fb">

易混词汇: memorize, remember, recall, recolect, <b>remind</b> 均有“记忆，记住，回忆”之意。
				<span class="stips">  </span>				<div class="snt_info"><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=memorize">memorize</a>: 指有意识的下功夫把某事的整个细节都记在脑子里。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=remember">remember</a>: 含义较广，多指无意识地回忆起往事，也可指通过主观努力去记忆。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=recall">recall</a>: 比remember文雅，指想方设法回忆已经遗忘之事。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=recolect">recolect</a>: 指在记忆中搜索，设法想起一时想不起的事情或人，强调过程。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=remind">remind</a>: 指经某人或某事的提醒而回忆起某件已遗忘之事。 				 				 
				 <div class="stips_fb">
				 <span class="tipsGood">好评</span> 
				 <span class="tipsBad">报错</span>

				<span class="stips">  </span>				<div class="snt_info"><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=special">special</a>: 普通用词，指不同于一般、与众不同，着重事物的专门性，突出与一般不同。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=especial">especial</a>: 和special含义很接近，较正式，但侧重有特殊的意义或重要性。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=specific">specific</a>: 着重指某种、某类事物具有的特殊或特定的属性，也可指专门提出作特别考虑的事物。 <br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=particular">particular</a>: 侧重不同于普遍性的个性或特殊性。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=exceptional">exceptional</a>: 指不同于一般，本身是特别的或异常的事物。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=extraordinary">extraordinary</a>: 语气比exceptional强，指极大地超过一般或正常情况。 <br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=peculiar">peculiar</a>: 强调指与众不同或独特的意思。

				<li class="error snt_hx" content="a bottle of _nc/_n" cate="e_noun.count.no_expected">[名词错误]			
 请检查<b>a bottle of .. champagne</b>，注意修饰语和名词可数性的一致性。
				<span class="stips">  </span>				<div class="snt_info">

				<li class="error_trp snt_hx" content="purchase" cate="confusion">[学习提示]			
易混词汇: buy, <b>purchase</b> 均含“购买”之意。
				<span class="stips">  </span>				<div class="snt_info"><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=buy">buy</a>: 普通日常用词，既可指日常随意购物也可指大的购买。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=purchase">purchase</a>: 正式用词，指大宗购货或购买重要东西。无感情色彩，强调物品的购得。 				 				 
				 <div class="stips_fb">
				 <span class="tipsGood">好评</span> 
				 <span class="tipsBad">报错</span>

				<li class="error_trp snt_hx" content="odd" cate="confusion">[学习提示]			
易混词汇: queer, <b>odd</b>, funny, crazy, curious, peculiar, strange, eccentric, quaint, singular 均含有“奇怪的，奇异的，新奇的”之意。
				<span class="stips">  </span>				<div class="snt_info"><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=queer">queer</a>: 指一种无法解释的怪诞，强调事物的奇特和不可思议。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=odd">odd</a>: 通常指不规律、偶尔出现的人或事物，往往令人困惑或奇怪。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=funny">funny</a>: 较通俗用词，指奇怪得滑稽可笑或反常。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=crazy">crazy</a>: 多指与众不同的行为、外表或人与物本身，含荒唐可笑或神经不正常的意味。 <br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=curious">curious</a>: 通常指非常特别或能引起注意、研究或探索的奇特。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=peculiar">peculiar</a>: 侧重令人奇怪的或独一无二的特性，也指性格特征方面显著的与众不同之处。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=strange">strange</a>: 普通常用词，含义广泛，指陌生新奇、奇怪、奇怪或不自然的人或物。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=eccentric">eccentric</a>: 指偏离常规的怪异或怪癖。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=quaint">quaint</a>: 指古色古香，会人感到既奇怪又有趣。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=singular">singular</a>: 通常指异常或奇特，暗含不同于一般。 				 				 
				 <div class="stips_fb">
				 <span class="tipsGood">好评</span> 
				 <span class="tipsBad">报错</span>

						<span>Intangible cultural heritages-第10号作文</span>

	 	<dt style="position:absolute;right:10px;top:-38px;"><a href="/index.php?c=v2&amp;a=view&amp;eid=55769766&amp;ds=pigai2&amp;order_eid="> 切换原文点评</a><sup style="color:red">New</sup></dt>

	<div id="myWriteContent">	
	 <div id="sponeLeft">
		<div id="etitle"> 
						<span id="swTitle">
			Intangible cultural heritages  			</span>
					</div><!-- end etitle -->

		<div id="sponeLeftT" style="width: 100%; overflow: hidden; outline: none;" tabindex="0">			 
			<div id="contentsW">

				<div id="contents">
																<div id="parahtml"><p id="p_1"><span id="s_0">Like tangible cultural heritages such as the Great Wall and the Forbidden City, intangible cultural heritages like Peking Opera and Confucius-commemorating rituals are equally crucial.</span><span id="s_1"> We should make our utmost efforts to preserve intangible heritages because, without their physical form of existence, they are in greater risk of extinction.</span><span id="s_2">According to UNESCO's Convention for the Safeguarding of Intangible Cultural Heritage (2003), all forms of social customs and habits, folklore, performing arts, rituals, oral traditions, festivals, traditional crafts and various knowledge and practices about nature and universe can be classified as intangible cultural heritages.</span><span id="s_3"> As a country consisting of a great diversity of ethnic groups and with time-honored history and civilization, China abounds in intangible cultural heritages.</span><span id="s_4"> Cultural heritages connect modern people with the historical past, allowing them to acquire a cultural and historical identity.</span><span id="s_5"> Without cultural heritages, we would be rendered absolutely rootless and we would find it hard to cope with challenges at present and in the future.</span><span id="s_6">However, the modernization process poses mounting threats to intangible heritages.</span><span id="s_7"> Many people have a blind faith in the latest electronic devices.</span><span id="s_8"> It is also pathetic to see elderly people in possession of such legacies pass away without transmitting them to the younger generation.</span><span id="s_9"> Faced with those challenges, we should both preserve and renovate our ancestral heritages so that we can help contribute to the cultural diversity of the world and return to our spiritual homeland in this age of impersonal science and technology.</span></p></div>
								
												</div>				
			</div>			 
		</div><!-- end sponeLeftT -->
		<div id="myWriteToolLine"></div>

				<li class="error_trp snt_hx" content="because" cate="i_suggest.word">[推荐表达]			
as/due to/since/as to/in that/for the reason that/for与短语<b>because</b> 意思相近，as/due to/since/as to/in that/for the reason that/for 更地道，推荐使用。

				<!-- zy add -->
								  
				<li class="error_trp snt_hx" content="consist of _n/vpat" cate="i_tip">[拓展辨析]			
注意<a href="http://bbs.pigai.org/t14342-1-1.html" target="_blank"><b>consist of</b>和<b>consist in</b>，<b>contain</b></a>区别。
				<span class="stips">  </span>				<div class="snt_info">consist of和consist in均为短语动词，但consist of表示“由……组成”[be made up of]；而consist in却表示“在于”[lie in]。
短语动词consist of表示“由……组成”[be made up of]，其宾语须是各个组成部分；而及物动词contain表示“包含”，“含有”[have within itself]，其宾语可只是部分组成部分。 				 				 
				 <div class="stips_fb">
				 <span class="tipsGood">好评</span> 
				 <span class="tipsBad">报错</span> 
				 <!--
				  
				 -->
				 </div>
				 				 
				</div>

				 <div class="stips_fb">
				 <span class="tipsGood">好评</span> 
				 <span class="tipsBad">报错</span> 
				 <!--
				  
				 -->
				 </div>
				 				 
				</div>
				</li>
				 								  
				<li class="error_trp snt_hx" content="world" cate="confusion">[学习提示]			
易混词汇: earth, <b>world</b>, globe 均可表示“地球”之意。
				<span class="stips">  </span>				<div class="snt_info"><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=earth">earth</a>: 指表面有陆地和水，人类所居住行星的名字。有时与“天”相对，泛指“地”。 <br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=world">world</a>: 通常相当于earth与globe，现多用指地球，地球上的世界，社会和人。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=globe">globe</a>: 指我们生活的地球，但强调其实体和圆形。 				 				 
				 <div class="stips_fb">
				 <span class="tipsGood">好评</span> 
				 <span class="tipsBad">报错</span> 
				 <!--
				  
				 -->
				 </div>
				 				 
				</div>
				</li>
				 				
								
				 

				

			   </ul>
			</div>
			<!-- end view3Error -->
			<div style="clear:both;"></div>
		</div>
		<!-- end view3Itme -->

			<div class="view3dx">第1段</div>

																<div id="parahtml"><p id="p_1"><span id="s_0">For most students of the universities, it is essential to get to know of the world outside the campus.</span><span id="s_1"> With the social development, the faster the social pace, the greater the knowledge of society we need, so that we must get to know the world.</span><span id="s_2"> Which way can we know of the world by?</span><span id="s_3"> There are many ways to be done.</span><span id="s_4"> First, we can know by the media, and the media is the most common of all and best.</span><span id="s_5"> Second, we can go out of campus to make any social service for people, by thus , we can get knowledge increasingly.</span><span id="s_6"> Of course, there're many other ways to be adopted.</span><span id="s_7"> As a student of university I intend to do some home teaching in my spare time, and to find some social jobs to do on holidays.</span><span id="s_8"> In addition, I'll take an active part in actions organized by my department or university ,etc.</span></p></div>

				<li class="error_trp snt_hx" content="essential" cate="confusion">[学习提示]			
易混词汇: basic, <b>essential</b>, fundamental, radical, vital 均有“基本的，基础的”之意。
				<span class="stips">  </span>				<div class="snt_info"><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=basic">basic</a>: 普通用词，指明确、具体的基础或起点。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=essential">essential</a>: 语气比basic和fundamental强，强调必不可少，暗含某物如缺少某部分，则失去本质特征的意味。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=fundamental">fundamental</a>: 书面用词，不如basic使用广泛，侧重指作为基础、根本的抽象的事物。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=radical">radical</a>: 着重指事物的根本或其来源。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=vital">vital</a>: 正式用词，侧重指维持生命、活力必不可少的，或生死攸关的。 				 				 
				 <div class="stips_fb">
				 <span class="tipsGood">好评</span> 
				 <span class="tipsBad">报错</span>

				<span class="stips">  </span>				<div class="snt_info"><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=earth">earth</a>: 指表面有陆地和水，人类所居住行星的名字。有时与“天”相对，泛指“地”。 <br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=world">world</a>: 通常相当于earth与globe，现多用指地球，地球上的世界，社会和人。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=globe">globe</a>: 指我们生活的地球，但强调其实体和圆形。

				<li class="error_trp snt_hx" content="common" cate="confusion">[学习提示]			
易混词汇: <b>common</b>, ordinary, commonplace, general, usual, popular, universal 均含有“普通的，普遍的”之意。
				<span class="stips">  </span>				<div class="snt_info"><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=common">common</a>: 多用于指物，侧重很常见，不稀奇。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=ordinary">ordinary</a>: 用于物，指每天发生，十分平淡无奇；用于人，指无特别之处，很一般。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=commonplace">commonplace</a>: 强调缺少新意。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=general">general</a>: 语气强于common，侧重大多如此，很少有例外情况。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=usual">usual</a>: 指常见常闻和常做的事或举动，强调惯常性。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=popular">popular</a>: 指适应大众爱好、需要，为大家所公认或接受。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=universal">universal</a>: 与general同义，但语气较强，侧重对每个人或事物都适用，根本没有例外。 				 				 
				 <div class="stips_fb">
				 <span class="tipsGood">好评</span> 
				 <span class="tipsBad">报错</span> 
				 <!--
				  
				 -->
				 </div>
				 				 
				</div>
				</li>
				 				
								
				 

				

			   </ul>
			</div>

				<!-- zy add -->
								  
				<li class="warn snt_hx" content="the normal economic world/_n" cate="w_chunk.oov_gramc._n">[搭配警示]			
搭配 <b>the normal economic world</b>在语料库中无此用法，疑似中式英语。
				<span class="stips">  </span>				<div class="snt_info">				 				 
				 <div class="stips_fb">
				 <span class="tipsGood">好评</span> 
				 <span class="tipsBad">报错</span> 
				 <!--
				  
				 -->
				 </div>
				 				 
				</div>
				</li>
				 								  
				<li class="error_trp snt_hx" content="world" cate="confusion">[学习提示]			
易混词汇: earth, <b>world</b>, globe 均可表示“地球”之意。
				<span class="stips">  </span>				<div class="snt_info"><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=earth">earth</a>: 指表面有陆地和水，人类所居住行星的名字。有时与“天”相对，泛指“地”。 <br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=world">world</a>: 通常相当于earth与globe，现多用指地球，地球上的世界，社会和人。<br /><a href="http://www.jukuu.com/search.php?q=globe">globe</a>: 指我们生活的地球，但强调其实体和圆形。 				 				 
				 <div class="stips_fb">
				 <span class="tipsGood">好评</span> 
				 <span class="tipsBad">报错</span> 
				 <!--
				  
				 -->
				 </div>
				 				 
				</div>
